  45          f.delete();

6190     private static boolean chkFile()
6191     {
6192         File javaFile=new File("LTTest_java.txt");
6193         if (! javaFile.exists())
6194         {
6195             System.out.println("FAIL:Failed to open file LTTest_java.txt - file not exists!");
6196             return false;
6197         }
6198         File cFile=new File("LTTest_c.txt");
6199         if (! cFile.exists())
6200         {
6201                 System.out.println("FAIL:Failed to open file LTTest_c.txt - file not exists!");
6202                 return false;
6203         }
6204         if ( cFile.length()!=javaFile.length() )
6205         {
6206             System.out.println("FAIL:File length not equal!");
6207             return false;
6208         }
6209         long byteCount=cFile.length();
6210         try{
6211             FileInputStream fisC=new FileInputStream(cFile);
6212             FileInputStream fisJava=new FileInputStream(javaFile);
6213             byte[] cData=new byte[fisC.available()];
6214             fisC.read(cData);
6215             byte[] javaData=new byte[fisJava.available()];
6216             fisJava.read(javaData);
6217             for ( int cnt=0;cnt<byteCount;++cnt)
6218             {
6219                 if ( cData[cnt]!=javaData[cnt] )
6220                 {
6221                     System.out.println("FAIL:Test failed! "+cnt+" byte are wrong! C file - " + cData[cnt] + " Java file - "+javaData[cnt] );
6222                     return false;
6223                 }
6224             }
6225         }
6226         catch (FileNotFoundException ex)
6227         {
6228             System.out.println("FAIL:Some of files not found!");
6229             return false;
6230         }
6231         catch (IOException ex)
6232         {
6233             System.out.println("FAIL:Failed to read files!");
6234             return false;
6235         }
6236         System.out.println("PASS: all data passed correctly!");
6237         return true;
6238     }
